const HEATMAP_GRADIENT = {
  0.2: '#ffe3b3',
  0.45: '#ffb347',
  0.7: '#ff8c42',
  1.0: '#ff5a1f',
};
const HEATMAP_RANGE_OPTIONS = ['1h', '6h', '24h'] as const;
type HeatmapRange = typeof HEATMAP_RANGE_OPTIONS[number];

interface MapViewportState {
  maxX: number;
  maxY: number;
  minX: number;
  minY: number;
  zoom: number;
}

interface HeatmapPayloadState {
  heatPoints: DashboardHeatPoint[];
  highlights: DashboardHeatHighlights;
  topFallaIds: string[];
  updatedAt: string | null;
}

interface ClusteredMapItem {
  fallas: Falla[];
  hasPrize: boolean;
  id: string;
  kind: 'cluster';
  lat: number;
  lng: number;
}

interface SingleMapItem {
  falla: Falla;
  id: string;
  kind: 'falla';
}

type RenderedMapItem = ClusteredMapItem | SingleMapItem;

function formatHeatTimestamp(value: string | null): string | null {
  if (!value) {
    return null;
  }

  const parsed = new Date(value);
  if (Number.isNaN(parsed.getTime())) {
    return null;
  }

  return parsed.toLocaleTimeString('es-ES', {
    hour: '2-digit',
    minute: '2-digit',
  });
}

function emptyHeatHighlights(): DashboardHeatHighlights {
  return {
    hottestZoneLabel: null,
    topFalla: null,
    topNeighborhood: null,
  };
}

function getHeatmapVisualOptions(zoom: number): L.HeatLayerOptions {
  if (zoom >= 16) {
    return {
      radius: 14,
      blur: 20,
      minOpacity: 0.1,
      maxZoom: 17,
      pane: 'heatmapPane',
      gradient: HEATMAP_GRADIENT,
    };
  }

  if (zoom >= 14) {
    return {
      radius: 20,
      blur: 26,
      minOpacity: 0.15,
      maxZoom: 17,
      pane: 'heatmapPane',
      gradient: HEATMAP_GRADIENT,
    };
  }

  return {
    radius: 28,
    blur: 30,
    minOpacity: 0.2,
    maxZoom: 17,
    pane: 'heatmapPane',
    gradient: HEATMAP_GRADIENT,
  };
}

function HeatmapLayer({
  enabled,
  points,
}: {
  enabled: boolean;
  points: DashboardHeatPoint[];
}) {
  const map = useMap();
  const layerRef = useRef<L.HeatLayer | null>(null);
  const applyVisualOptions = useCallback(() => {
    if (!layerRef.current) {
      return;
    }

    layerRef.current.setOptions(getHeatmapVisualOptions(map.getZoom()));
  }, [map]);

  useMapEvents({
    zoomend: applyVisualOptions,
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!enabled || points.length === 0) {
      if (layerRef.current && map.hasLayer(layerRef.current)) {
        map.removeLayer(layerRef.current);
      }
      return;
    }

    const latLngs = points.map((point) => [point.lat, point.lng, point.intensity] as [number, number, number]);

    if (!layerRef.current) {
      layerRef.current = L.heatLayer(latLngs, {
        ...getHeatmapVisualOptions(map.getZoom()),
      });
    } else {
      layerRef.current.setLatLngs(latLngs);
      layerRef.current.setOptions(getHeatmapVisualOptions(map.getZoom()));
    }

    if (!map.hasLayer(layerRef.current)) {
      layerRef.current.addTo(map);
    }
  }, [enabled, map, points]);

  useEffect(() => () => {
    if (layerRef.current && map.hasLayer(layerRef.current)) {
      map.removeLayer(layerRef.current);
    }
    layerRef.current = null;
  }, [map]);

  return null;
}

function HeatmapDataBridge({
  enabled,
  onLoadingChange,
  onPayloadChange,
  range,
}: {
  enabled: boolean;
  onLoadingChange: (value: boolean) => void;
  onPayloadChange: (payload: HeatmapPayloadState) => void;
  range: HeatmapRange;
}) {
  const map = useMap();
  const abortRef = useRef<AbortController | null>(null);
  const timeoutRef = useRef<number | null>(null);
  const requestIdRef = useRef(0);

  const clearPendingRequest = useCallback(() => {
    if (timeoutRef.current !== null) {
      window.clearTimeout(timeoutRef.current);
      timeoutRef.current = null;
    }

    if (abortRef.current) {
      abortRef.current.abort();
      abortRef.current = null;
    }
  }, []);

  const loadHeatmap = useCallback(() => {
    if (!enabled) {
      clearPendingRequest();
      onLoadingChange(false);
      onPayloadChange({
        heatPoints: [],
        highlights: emptyHeatHighlights(),
        topFallaIds: [],
        updatedAt: null,
      });
      return;
    }

    clearPendingRequest();

    timeoutRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
      const bounds = map.getBounds();
      const bbox = [
        bounds.getSouth(),
        bounds.getWest(),
        bounds.getNorth(),
        bounds.getEast(),
      ].join(',');

      const controller = new AbortController();
      const requestId = requestIdRef.current + 1;
      requestIdRef.current = requestId;
      abortRef.current = controller;
      onLoadingChange(true);

      fetchDashboardHeatmap(bbox, map.getZoom(), range, controller.signal)
        .then((payload) => {
          if (requestId !== requestIdRef.current) {
            return;
          }

          onPayloadChange(payload);
        })
        .catch((error) => {
          if (controller.signal.aborted) {
            return;
          }

          if (error instanceof Error && error.message === 'SESSION_INVALID') {
            const pathname = window.location.pathname;
            const dashboardIndex = pathname.indexOf('/dashboard');
            const basePath = dashboardIndex === -1 ? '' : pathname.slice(0, dashboardIndex);
            window.location.replace(`${basePath}/login.php`);
            return;
          }

          if (requestId === requestIdRef.current) {
            onPayloadChange({
              heatPoints: [],
              highlights: emptyHeatHighlights(),
              topFallaIds: [],
              updatedAt: null,
            });
          }
        })
        .finally(() => {
          if (requestId === requestIdRef.current) {
            onLoadingChange(false);
          }
        });
    }, 180);
  }, [clearPendingRequest, enabled, map, onLoadingChange, onPayloadChange, range]);

  useMapEvents({
    moveend: loadHeatmap,
    resize: loadHeatmap,
    zoomend: loadHeatmap,
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    loadHeatmap();

    if (!enabled) {
      return () => {
        clearPendingRequest();
        onLoadingChange(false);
      };
    }

    const intervalId = window.setInterval(() => {
      loadHeatmap();
    }, 30000);

    return () => {
      window.clearInterval(intervalId);
      clearPendingRequest();
      onLoadingChange(false);
    };
  }, [clearPendingRequest, enabled, loadHeatmap, onLoadingChange]);

  return null;
}
function createFallaIcon(selected: boolean, active: boolean, prize?: number, trending = false) {
  const hasPrize = typeof prize === 'number';
  const bg = selected ? '#0f172a' : active ? '#ff6321' : hasPrize ? 'linear-gradient(180deg,#fff2b8 0%,#f5b942 100%)' : '#ffffff';
  const fg = selected || active ? '#ffffff' : hasPrize ? '#8a4b00' : '#ff6321';
  const badge = prize ? `#${prize}` : active ? 'Ruta' : null;
  const badgeHtml = badge
    ? `<div class="absolute -top-8 rounded-full bg-white/92 px-2.5 py-1 text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-slate-700 shadow-[0_12px_28px_rgba(15,23,42,0.12)]">${badge}</div>`
    : '';
  const trendingHalo = trending
    ? '<div class="absolute h-[4.15rem] w-[4.15rem] rounded-full" style="background:rgba(255,122,26,0.08);box-shadow:0 0 0 5px rgba(255,122,26,0.16);"></div>'
    : '';
  const iconHtml = hasPrize
    ? `
        <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round">
          <path d="M8 4h8v3a4 4 0 0 1-8 0z"/>
          <path d="M9 18h6"/>
          <path d="M10 15h4v3h-4z"/>
          <path d="M16 5h2a1 1 0 0 1 1 1 4 4 0 0 1-4 4"/>
          <path d="M8 5H6a1 1 0 0 0-1 1 4 4 0 0 0 4 4"/>
        </svg>
      `
    : `
        <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round">
          <path d="M8.5 14.5A2.5 2.5 0 0 0 11 12c0-1.38-.5-2-1-3-1.072-2.143-.224-4.054 2-6 .5 2.5 2 4.5 3.5 6.5 1.5 2 2 4.5 2 7a2.5 2.5 0 0 1-5 0c0-1.38-.5-2-1-3-1.072-2.143-.224-4.054-2-6 .5 2.5 2 4.5 3.5 6.5 1.5 2 2 4.5 2 7a2.5 2.5 0 0 1-5 0z"/>
        </svg>
      `;

  return new L.DivIcon({
    className: 'falla-map-marker',
    html: `
      <div class="relative flex items-center justify-center">
        ${badgeHtml}
        ${trendingHalo}
        <div class="absolute h-14 w-14 rounded-full blur-[2px]" style="background:${selected ? 'rgba(15,23,42,0.26)' : active ? 'rgba(255,99,33,0.24)' : hasPrize ? 'rgba(245,185,66,0.3)' : 'rgba(255,99,33,0.18)'};"></div>
        <div class="relative flex h-12 w-12 items-center justify-center rounded-[1.45rem] border-2 shadow-[0_20px_38px_rgba(15,23,42,0.14)]" style="background:${bg};color:${fg};border-color:${selected || active ? '#ffffff' : hasPrize ? '#fcd34d' : '#ffffff'};">
          ${iconHtml}
        </div>
      </div>
    `,
    iconSize: [56, 66],
    iconAnchor: [28, 38],
  });
}

function getCachedFallaIcon(selected: boolean, active: boolean, prize?: number, trending = false) {
  const cacheKey = `${selected ? '1' : '0'}:${active ? '1' : '0'}:${trending ? '1' : '0'}:${typeof prize === 'number' ? prize : 'none'}`;
  const cachedIcon = FALLA_ICON_CACHE.get(cacheKey);

  if (cachedIcon) {
    return cachedIcon;
  }

  const nextIcon = createFallaIcon(selected, active, prize, trending);
  FALLA_ICON_CACHE.set(cacheKey, nextIcon);
  return nextIcon;
}

function createClusterIcon(count: number, hasPrize: boolean) {
  const background = hasPrize ? 'linear-gradient(180deg,#ffe59c 0%,#f5b942 100%)' : 'linear-gradient(180deg,#ffffff 0%,#fff3eb 100%)';
  const border = hasPrize ? '#f4b534' : '#ffd2bf';
  const text = hasPrize ? '#7c3f00' : '#ff6321';

  return new L.DivIcon({
    className: 'falla-map-cluster',
    html: `
      <div class="relative flex items-center justify-center">
        <div class="absolute h-16 w-16 rounded-full blur-[2px]" style="background:${hasPrize ? 'rgba(245,185,66,0.28)' : 'rgba(255,99,33,0.18)'};"></div>
        <div class="relative flex h-14 w-14 items-center justify-center rounded-full border-2 shadow-[0_18px_36px_rgba(15,23,42,0.14)]" style="background:${background};border-color:${border};color:${text};">
          <span class="text-[12px] font-black tracking-[0.04em]">${count}</span>
        </div>
      </div>
    `,
    iconSize: [60, 60],
    iconAnchor: [30, 30],
  });
}

function getCachedClusterIcon(count: number, hasPrize: boolean) {
  const cacheKey = `${count}:${hasPrize ? '1' : '0'}`;
  const cachedIcon = CLUSTER_ICON_CACHE.get(cacheKey);

  if (cachedIcon) {
    return cachedIcon;
  }

  const nextIcon = createClusterIcon(count, hasPrize);
  CLUSTER_ICON_CACHE.set(cacheKey, nextIcon);
  return nextIcon;
}

function readMapViewportState(map: L.Map): MapViewportState {
  const pixelBounds = map.getPixelBounds();

  return {
    minX: pixelBounds.min.x,
    minY: pixelBounds.min.y,
    maxX: pixelBounds.max.x,
    maxY: pixelBounds.max.y,
    zoom: map.getZoom(),
  };
}

function MapViewportBridge({
  onChange,
}: {
  onChange: (state: MapViewportState) => void;
}) {
  const map = useMapEvents({
    moveend: () => onChange(readMapViewportState(map)),
    resize: () => onChange(readMapViewportState(map)),
    zoomend: () => onChange(readMapViewportState(map)),
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    onChange(readMapViewportState(map));
  }, [map, onChange]);

  return null;
}

function ViewportController({
  fallas,
  selectedFalla,
  activeRouteFalla,
  clusterFocusFallas,
  userPosition,
  focusClusterToken,
  focusUserToken,
  focusSelectedToken,
  onBackgroundClick,
}: {
  fallas: Falla[];
  selectedFalla: Falla | null;
  activeRouteFalla: Falla | null;
  clusterFocusFallas: Falla[] | null;
  userPosition: MapPoint | null;
  focusClusterToken: number;
  focusUserToken: number;
  focusSelectedToken: number;
  onBackgroundClick: () => void;
}) {
  const map = useMap();
  const lastAutoFitKey = useRef<string>('');
  useMapEvents({ click: onBackgroundClick });

  useEffect(() => {
    map.invalidateSize();
  }, [fallas.length, map]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!selectedFalla) {
      return;
    }

    lastAutoFitKey.current = `selected:${selectedFalla.id}`;
    map.flyTo([selectedFalla.lat, selectedFalla.lng], map.getSize().x < 640 ? 15 : 16, { duration: 0.85 });
  }, [map, selectedFalla]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!(activeRouteFalla && userPosition)) {
      return;
    }

    const routeKey = `route:${activeRouteFalla.id}:${userPosition[0].toFixed(5)}:${userPosition[1].toFixed(5)}`;
    if (lastAutoFitKey.current === routeKey) {
      return;
    }

    lastAutoFitKey.current = routeKey;
    map.fitBounds([userPosition, [activeRouteFalla.lat, activeRouteFalla.lng]], {
      paddingTopLeft: L.point(28, 28),
      paddingBottomRight: L.point(28, map.getSize().x < 1024 ? 220 : 120),
      maxZoom: 15,
    });
  }, [activeRouteFalla, map, userPosition]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (selectedFalla || activeRouteFalla || fallas.length === 0) {
      return;
    }

    const visibleKey = `visible:${fallas.map((falla) => falla.id).join(',')}`;
    if (lastAutoFitKey.current === visibleKey) {
      return;
    }

    lastAutoFitKey.current = visibleKey;

    if (fallas.length === 1) {
      map.flyTo([fallas[0].lat, fallas[0].lng], map.getSize().x < 640 ? 14 : 15, { duration: 0.8 });
      return;
    }

    map.fitBounds(fallas.map((falla) => [falla.lat, falla.lng] as MapPoint), {
      paddingTopLeft: L.point(28, 28),
      paddingBottomRight: L.point(28, map.getSize().x < 1024 ? 180 : 48),
      maxZoom: 14,
    });
  }, [activeRouteFalla, fallas, map, selectedFalla, userPosition]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!focusClusterToken || !clusterFocusFallas?.length) {
      return;
    }

    if (clusterFocusFallas.length === 1) {
      const [target] = clusterFocusFallas;
      map.flyTo([target.lat, target.lng], map.getSize().x < 640 ? 15 : 16, { duration: 0.75 });
      return;
    }

    map.fitBounds(clusterFocusFallas.map((falla) => [falla.lat, falla.lng] as MapPoint), {
      paddingTopLeft: L.point(28, 28),
      paddingBottomRight: L.point(28, map.getSize().x < 1024 ? 220 : 120),
      maxZoom: 16,
    });
  }, [clusterFocusFallas, focusClusterToken, map]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (focusUserToken && userPosition) {
      lastAutoFitKey.current = `user:${userPosition[0].toFixed(5)}:${userPosition[1].toFixed(5)}`;
      map.flyTo(userPosition, 16, { duration: 0.9 });
    }
  }, [focusUserToken, map, userPosition]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const target = selectedFalla ?? activeRouteFalla;
    if (focusSelectedToken && target) {
      map.flyTo([target.lat, target.lng], map.getSize().x < 640 ? 15 : 16, { duration: 0.9 });
    }
  }, [activeRouteFalla, focusSelectedToken, map, selectedFalla]);

  return null;
}

interface FallaMapProps {
  isDarkMode: boolean;
  variant?: 'default' | 'expanded';
  frameClassName?: string;
  mapHeightClassName?: string;
  heatmapEnabled?: boolean;
  setHeatmapEnabled?: (enabled: boolean) => void;
  mapStyleId: MapStyleId;
  setMapStyleId: (value: MapStyleId) => void;
  mapSearchQuery: string;
  setMapSearchQuery: (value: string) => void;
  onOpenExpandedMap?: () => void;
  activeRouteFalla: Falla | null;
  activeRouteFallaId: string | null;
  setActiveRouteFallaId: (value: string | null) => void;
  fallas: Falla[];
  selectedFalla: Falla | null;
  setSelectedFalla: (value: Falla | null) => void;
  userPosition: MapPoint | null;
  locationStatus: LocationStatus;
  requestLocation: () => Promise<MapPoint>;
  favorites: string[];
  toggleFavorite: (id: string, event?: React.MouseEvent) => void;
  onShowDetail: (falla: Falla) => void;
  onPrepareRoute: (falla: Falla) => void;
}

function FallaMapComponent({
  isDarkMode,
  variant = 'default',
  frameClassName,
  mapHeightClassName,
  heatmapEnabled,
  setHeatmapEnabled,
  mapStyleId,
  setMapStyleId,
  mapSearchQuery,
  setMapSearchQuery,
  onOpenExpandedMap,
  activeRouteFalla,
  activeRouteFallaId,
  setActiveRouteFallaId,
  fallas,
  selectedFalla,
  setSelectedFalla,
  userPosition,
  locationStatus,
  requestLocation,
  favorites,
  toggleFavorite,
  onShowDetail,
  onPrepareRoute,
}: FallaMapProps) {
  const [focusUserToken, setFocusUserToken] = useState(0);
  const [focusSelectedToken, setFocusSelectedToken] = useState(0);
  const [focusClusterToken, setFocusClusterToken] = useState(0);
  const [isLocating, setIsLocating] = useState(false);
  const [isControlsVisible, setIsControlsVisible] = useState(false);
  const [isIntroVisible, setIsIntroVisible] = useState(false);
  const [isHeatmapEnabledInternal, setIsHeatmapEnabledInternal] = useState(false);
  const [hasActivatedHeatmap, setHasActivatedHeatmap] = useState(false);
  const [isHeatmapLoading, setIsHeatmapLoading] = useState(false);
  const [heatmapRange, setHeatmapRange] = useState<HeatmapRange>('1h');
  const [heatmapPayload, setHeatmapPayload] = useState<HeatmapPayloadState>({
    heatPoints: [],
    highlights: emptyHeatHighlights(),
    topFallaIds: [],
    updatedAt: null,
  });
  const [clusterFocusFallas, setClusterFocusFallas] = useState<Falla[] | null>(null);
  const [viewportState, setViewportState] = useState<MapViewportState | null>(null);
  const activeTheme = useMemo(() => getMapTheme(mapStyleId), [mapStyleId]);
  const isDarkTheme = isDarkMode || activeTheme.id !== 'city';
  const isHeatmapEnabled = heatmapEnabled ?? isHeatmapEnabledInternal;
  const commitHeatmapEnabled = setHeatmapEnabled ?? setIsHeatmapEnabledInternal;
  const trendingFallaIdSet = useMemo(() => new Set(heatmapPayload.topFallaIds), [heatmapPayload.topFallaIds]);
  const heatmapUpdatedLabel = useMemo(() => formatHeatTimestamp(heatmapPayload.updatedAt), [heatmapPayload.updatedAt]);
  const heatmapSummary = heatmapPayload.highlights;
  const deferredMapSearchQuery = useDeferredValue(mapSearchQuery);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (isHeatmapEnabled) {
      setHasActivatedHeatmap(true);
    }
  }, [isHeatmapEnabled]);
  const normalizedMapSearch = deferredMapSearchQuery.trim().toLowerCase();
  const visibleFallas = useMemo(() => {
    if (!normalizedMapSearch) {
      return fallas;
    }

    return fallas.filter((falla) => (
      `${falla.name} ${falla.neighborhood} ${falla.section} ${falla.artist} ${falla.address ?? ''}`
        .toLowerCase()
        .includes(normalizedMapSearch)
    ));
  }, [fallas, normalizedMapSearch]);
  const displayedFallas = useMemo(() => {
    const items = [...visibleFallas];

    if (selectedFalla && !items.some((item) => item.id === selectedFalla.id)) {
      items.unshift(selectedFalla);
    }

    if (activeRouteFalla && !items.some((item) => item.id === activeRouteFalla.id)) {
      items.unshift(activeRouteFalla);
    }

    return items.filter((item, index, array) => array.findIndex((candidate) => candidate.id === item.id) === index);
  }, [activeRouteFalla, selectedFalla, visibleFallas]);
  const quickFallas = useMemo(() => {
    const source = userPosition
      ? [...visibleFallas].sort((a, b) => distanceBetweenPoints(userPosition, [a.lat, a.lng]) - distanceBetweenPoints(userPosition, [b.lat, b.lng]))
      : [...visibleFallas].sort((a, b) => (a.prize ?? 99) - (b.prize ?? 99) || b.likes - a.likes);
    return source.slice(0, 3);
  }, [userPosition, visibleFallas]);
  const handleViewportChange = useCallback((nextState: MapViewportState) => {
    setViewportState((current) => {
      if (
        current
        && current.zoom === nextState.zoom
        && current.minX === nextState.minX
        && current.minY === nextState.minY
        && current.maxX === nextState.maxX
        && current.maxY === nextState.maxY
      ) {
        return current;
      }

      return nextState;
    });
  }, []);
  const handleMarkerSelect = useCallback((falla: Falla) => {
    setClusterFocusFallas(null);
    setSelectedFalla(falla);
    setFocusSelectedToken((current) => current + 1);
    trackActivityEvent({
      eventType: 'marker_open',
      fallaId: falla.id,
      latitude: falla.lat,
      longitude: falla.lng,
    });
  }, [setSelectedFalla]);
  const handleShowDetail = useCallback((falla: Falla) => {
    trackActivityEvent({
      eventType: 'detail_open',
      fallaId: falla.id,
      latitude: falla.lat,
      longitude: falla.lng,
    });
    onShowDetail(falla);
  }, [onShowDetail]);
  const handlePrepareRoute = useCallback((falla: Falla) => {
    trackActivityEvent({
      eventType: 'route_prepare',
      fallaId: falla.id,
      latitude: falla.lat,
      longitude: falla.lng,
    });
    onPrepareRoute(falla);
  }, [onPrepareRoute]);
  const handleFavoriteToggle = useCallback((falla: Falla, event?: React.MouseEvent) => {
    trackActivityEvent({
      eventType: 'favorite_toggle',
      fallaId: falla.id,
      latitude: falla.lat,
      longitude: falla.lng,
    });
    toggleFavorite(falla.id, event);
  }, [toggleFavorite]);
  const renderedMapItems = useMemo<RenderedMapItem[]>(() => {
    if (!viewportState) {
      return displayedFallas.map((falla) => ({ kind: 'falla', id: falla.id, falla }));
    }

    const zoom = viewportState.zoom;
    const padding = zoom >= 16 ? 80 : zoom >= 14 ? 120 : 160;
    const minX = viewportState.minX - padding;
    const minY = viewportState.minY - padding;
    const maxX = viewportState.maxX + padding;
    const maxY = viewportState.maxY + padding;
    const cellSize = zoom >= 16 ? 0 : zoom >= 15 ? 54 : zoom >= 14 ? 64 : 76;
    const pinnedIds = new Set(
      [selectedFalla?.id, activeRouteFalla?.id].filter((value): value is string => Boolean(value))
    );
    const clusters = new Map<string, { fallas: Falla[]; latSum: number; lngSum: number; hasPrize: boolean }>();
    const items: RenderedMapItem[] = [];

    for (const falla of displayedFallas) {
      if (pinnedIds.has(falla.id)) {
        items.push({ kind: 'falla', id: falla.id, falla });
        continue;
      }

      const point = L.CRS.EPSG3857.latLngToPoint(L.latLng(falla.lat, falla.lng), zoom);
      if (point.x < minX || point.x > maxX || point.y < minY || point.y > maxY) {
        continue;
      }

      if (cellSize === 0) {
        items.push({ kind: 'falla', id: falla.id, falla });
        continue;
      }

      const bucketX = Math.floor((point.x - minX) / cellSize);
      const bucketY = Math.floor((point.y - minY) / cellSize);
      const bucketKey = `${bucketX}:${bucketY}`;
      const bucket = clusters.get(bucketKey);

      if (bucket) {
        bucket.fallas.push(falla);
        bucket.latSum += falla.lat;
        bucket.lngSum += falla.lng;
        bucket.hasPrize = bucket.hasPrize || typeof falla.prize === 'number';
      } else {
        clusters.set(bucketKey, {
          fallas: [falla],
          latSum: falla.lat,
          lngSum: falla.lng,
          hasPrize: typeof falla.prize === 'number',
        });
      }
    }

    clusters.forEach((cluster, bucketKey) => {
      if (cluster.fallas.length === 1) {
        items.push({ kind: 'falla', id: cluster.fallas[0].id, falla: cluster.fallas[0] });
        return;
      }

      items.push({
        kind: 'cluster',
        id: `cluster:${zoom}:${bucketKey}:${cluster.fallas.length}`,
        lat: cluster.latSum / cluster.fallas.length,
        lng: cluster.lngSum / cluster.fallas.length,
        fallas: cluster.fallas,
        hasPrize: cluster.hasPrize,
      });
    });

    return items;
  }, [activeRouteFalla?.id, displayedFallas, selectedFalla?.id, viewportState]);
  const markerNodes = useMemo(() => (
    renderedMapItems.map((item) => {
      if (item.kind === 'cluster') {
        return (
          <Marker
            key={item.id}
            position={[item.lat, item.lng]}
            icon={getCachedClusterIcon(item.fallas.length, item.hasPrize)}
            eventHandlers={{
              click: () => {
                setClusterFocusFallas(item.fallas);
                setFocusClusterToken((current) => current + 1);
              },
            }}
          />
        );
      }

      const falla = item.falla;
      return (
        <Marker
          key={falla.id}
          position={[falla.lat, falla.lng]}
          icon={getCachedFallaIcon(
            selectedFalla?.id === falla.id,
            activeRouteFallaId === falla.id,
            falla.prize,
            isHeatmapEnabled && trendingFallaIdSet.has(falla.id),
          )}
          eventHandlers={{ click: () => handleMarkerSelect(falla) }}
        />
      );
    })
  ), [activeRouteFallaId, handleMarkerSelect, isHeatmapEnabled, renderedMapItems, selectedFalla?.id, trendingFallaIdSet]);

  const locateUser = async () => {
    if (userPosition) {
      setFocusUserToken((current) => current + 1);
      return;
    }
    setIsLocating(true);
    try {
      await requestLocation();
      setFocusUserToken((current) => current + 1);
    } catch {
      // The badge already explains the status.
    } finally {
      setIsLocating(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <section
      className={cn(
        'relative overflow-hidden border shadow-[0_38px_100px_rgba(15,23,42,0.16)]',
        variant === 'expanded' ? 'rounded-[24px] p-3 sm:p-4' : 'rounded-[24px] p-3',
        isDarkMode
          ? 'border-white/10 bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.05),rgba(255,255,255,0.03))]'
          : 'border-white/80 bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_right,rgba(255,174,122,0.18),transparent_24%),linear-gradient(180deg,#fffaf6_0%,#f4eee6_100%)]'
        ,frameClassName
      )}
    >
      <div className="pointer-events-none absolute -right-10 -top-10 h-36 w-36 rounded-full bg-brand/12 blur-3xl" />
      <div
        className={cn(
          'relative overflow-hidden rounded-[24px]',
          mapHeightClassName ?? (variant === 'expanded' ? 'h-[min(84vh,1080px)] min-h-[760px]' : 'h-[min(76vh,900px)] min-h-[660px]')
        )}
      >
        <MapContainer
          center={DEFAULT_CENTER}
          zoom={13}
          zoomControl={false}
          scrollWheelZoom={true}
          preferCanvas={true}
          className="h-full w-full"
        >
          <TileLayer attribution={activeTheme.attribution} url={activeTheme.url} maxZoom={activeTheme.maxZoom ?? 20} />
          <ZoomControl position="topright" />
          <MapViewportBridge onChange={handleViewportChange} />
          <Pane name="heatmapPane" style={{ zIndex: 350, pointerEvents: 'none' }}>
            <HeatmapLayer enabled={isHeatmapEnabled} points={heatmapPayload.heatPoints} />
            <HeatmapDataBridge
              enabled={isHeatmapEnabled}
              onLoadingChange={setIsHeatmapLoading}
              onPayloadChange={setHeatmapPayload}
              range={heatmapRange}
            />
          </Pane>
          <Pane name="routePane" style={{ zIndex: 500 }}>
            {userPosition ? (
              <Circle
                center={userPosition}
                radius={90}
                pathOptions={{ color: '#38bdf8', fillColor: '#38bdf8', fillOpacity: 0.1, weight: 1.4, opacity: 0.55 }}
              />
            ) : null}
          </Pane>
          <Pane name="fallasPane" style={{ zIndex: 650 }}>
            {userPosition ? (
              <Marker position={userPosition} icon={USER_ICON} />
            ) : null}
            {markerNodes}
          </Pane>
          <ViewportController
            fallas={visibleFallas}
            selectedFalla={selectedFalla}
            activeRouteFalla={activeRouteFalla}
            clusterFocusFallas={clusterFocusFallas}
            userPosition={userPosition}
            focusClusterToken={focusClusterToken}
            focusUserToken={focusUserToken}
            focusSelectedToken={focusSelectedToken}
            onBackgroundClick={() => setSelectedFalla(null)}
          />
        </MapContainer>
        <div
          className={cn(
            'pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 z-[120]',
            isDarkTheme
              ? 'bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_left,rgba(255,255,255,0.03),transparent_28%),linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(2,6,23,0.1),rgba(2,6,23,0.03)_28%,rgba(2,6,23,0.12)_100%)]'
              : 'bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_left,rgba(255,255,255,0.2),transparent_30%),linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(255,248,238,0.14),rgba(255,248,238,0.04)_28%,rgba(255,255,255,0.12)_100%)]'
          )}
        />

        <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 z-[1000]">
          <div className="absolute inset-x-4 top-4 flex items-start justify-between gap-3 sm:inset-x-5 sm:top-5">
            {isControlsVisible ? (
            <div className={cn('pointer-events-auto rounded-[24px] border px-3 py-3 shadow-[0_20px_44px_rgba(15,23,42,0.15)] backdrop-blur-2xl', isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-slate-950/82 text-white' : 'border-white/80 bg-white/92 text-slate-950')}>
              <div className="mb-2 flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
                <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                  <span className={cn('inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em]', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-brand/16 text-brand' : 'bg-[#fff1e8] text-brand')}>
                    <Sparkles className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
                    Mapa en vivo
                  </span>
                  <span className={cn('hidden rounded-full px-3 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] md:inline-flex', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/70' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-500')}>
                    {activeTheme.label}
                  </span>
                </div>
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => setIsControlsVisible(false)}
                  className={cn('inline-flex h-9 w-9 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-[1rem] border transition-colors', isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-white/8 text-white hover:bg-white/12' : 'border-slate-100 bg-slate-100 text-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-200')}
                  aria-label="Ocultar controles"
                >
                  <X className="h-4 w-4" />
                </button>
              </div>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                <span className={cn('inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em]', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-white/10 text-white/80' : 'bg-[#fff1e8] text-brand')}><Layers3 className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />Capas</span>
                {MAP_THEMES.map((theme) => (
                  <button key={theme.id} type="button" onClick={() => setMapStyleId(theme.id)} className={cn('rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all', mapStyleId === theme.id ? 'bg-slate-950 text-white shadow-lg shadow-slate-950/20' : isDarkTheme ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/72 hover:bg-white/12' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-500 hover:bg-slate-200')}>
                    {theme.shortLabel}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
              <div className="mt-3 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => {
                    const nextValue = !isHeatmapEnabled;
                    if (nextValue) {
                      setHasActivatedHeatmap(true);
                    }
                    commitHeatmapEnabled(nextValue);
                  }}
                  className={cn(
                    'inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all',
                    isHeatmapEnabled
                      ? 'bg-brand text-white shadow-[0_14px_28px_rgba(255,99,33,0.24)]'
                      : isDarkTheme
                        ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/72 hover:bg-white/12'
                        : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-500 hover:bg-slate-200'
                  )}
                >
                  <Flame className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
                  {isHeatmapEnabled ? 'Actividad on' : 'Actividad'}
                </button>
                {HEATMAP_RANGE_OPTIONS.map((option) => (
                  <button
                    key={option}
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setHeatmapRange(option)}
                    disabled={!isHeatmapEnabled}
                    className={cn(
                      'rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-45',
                      heatmapRange === option
                        ? 'bg-slate-950 text-white shadow-lg shadow-slate-950/20'
                        : isDarkTheme
                          ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/72 hover:bg-white/12'
                          : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-500 hover:bg-slate-200'
                    )}
                  >
                    {option}
                  </button>
                ))}
                {heatmapUpdatedLabel ? (
                  <span className={cn('inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em]', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/64' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-500')}>
                    {isHeatmapLoading ? 'Actualizando' : `Heat ${heatmapUpdatedLabel}`}
                  </span>
                ) : isHeatmapLoading ? (
                  <span className={cn('inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em]', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/64' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-500')}>
                    Actualizando calor
                  </span>
                ) : null}
              </div>
              <div className={cn('mt-3 flex items-center gap-2 rounded-[1.2rem] border px-3 py-2.5 shadow-[0_14px_30px_rgba(15,23,42,0.08)]', isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/10 bg-white/6' : 'border-white/80 bg-white/92')}>
                <Search className={cn('h-4 w-4 shrink-0', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/55' : 'text-slate-400')} />
                <input
                  type="search"
                  value={mapSearchQuery}
                  onChange={(event) => setMapSearchQuery(event.target.value)}
                  placeholder="Busca falla, barrio o seccion"
                  className={cn('min-w-0 flex-1 bg-transparent text-[13px] font-bold outline-none placeholder:font-bold', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white placeholder:text-white/38' : 'text-slate-800 placeholder:text-slate-400')}
                />
                {mapSearchQuery ? (
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setMapSearchQuery('')}
                    className={cn('inline-flex h-8 w-8 items-center justify-center rounded-full transition-colors', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/70 hover:bg-white/12' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-500 hover:bg-slate-200')}
                    aria-label="Limpiar búsqueda"
                  >
                    <X className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </button>
                ) : null}
              </div>
            </div>
            ) : <div />}

            <div className="pointer-events-auto flex flex-wrap items-center justify-end gap-2">
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => setIsControlsVisible((current) => !current)}
                className={cn(
                  'pointer-events-auto inline-flex h-12 w-12 items-center justify-center rounded-[18px] border shadow-[0_18px_38px_rgba(15,23,42,0.12)] backdrop-blur-xl transition-colors',
                  isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-slate-950/80 text-white hover:bg-slate-900/90' : 'border-white/70 bg-white/92 text-slate-700 hover:bg-white'
                )}
                aria-label={isControlsVisible ? 'Ocultar controles del mapa' : 'Mostrar controles del mapa'}
              >
                <Layers3 className={cn('h-5 w-5', mapSearchQuery.trim() ? 'text-brand' : 'text-sky-500')} />
              </button>
              {variant === 'default' && onOpenExpandedMap ? (
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={onOpenExpandedMap}
                  className={cn('inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] shadow-[0_18px_38px_rgba(15,23,42,0.12)] backdrop-blur-xl transition-colors', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-slate-950/82 text-white hover:bg-slate-900/90' : 'bg-white/94 text-slate-700 hover:bg-white')}
                >
                  <Maximize2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-brand" />
                  Mapa amplio
                </button>
              ) : null}
              <span className={cn('inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] shadow-[0_18px_38px_rgba(15,23,42,0.12)] backdrop-blur-xl', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-slate-950/82 text-white' : 'bg-white/94 text-slate-700')}>{String(visibleFallas.length).padStart(2, '0')} visibles</span>
              <span className={cn('inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] shadow-[0_18px_38px_rgba(15,23,42,0.12)] backdrop-blur-xl', locationStatus === 'ready' ? 'bg-emerald-500 text-white' : locationStatus === 'blocked' || locationStatus === 'unsupported' ? 'bg-amber-500 text-slate-950' : isDarkTheme ? 'bg-slate-950/80 text-white' : 'bg-white/92 text-slate-700')}>
                <Navigation className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
                {locationStatus === 'ready' ? 'GPS activo' : locationStatus === 'loading' ? 'Buscando GPS' : locationStatus === 'blocked' ? 'GPS bloqueado' : 'Sin GPS'}
              </span>
              <button type="button" onClick={() => void locateUser()} className={cn('pointer-events-auto inline-flex h-12 w-12 items-center justify-center rounded-[1.2rem] border shadow-[0_18px_38px_rgba(15,23,42,0.12)] backdrop-blur-xl transition-colors', isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-slate-950/80 text-white hover:bg-slate-900/90' : 'border-white/70 bg-white/92 text-slate-700 hover:bg-white')}>
                <LocateFixed className={cn('h-5 w-5', isLocating && 'animate-pulse')} />
              </button>
              {selectedFalla && (
                <button type="button" onClick={() => setSelectedFalla(null)} className={cn('pointer-events-auto inline-flex h-12 w-12 items-center justify-center rounded-[1.2rem] border shadow-[0_18px_38px_rgba(15,23,42,0.12)] backdrop-blur-xl transition-colors', isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-slate-950/80 text-white hover:bg-slate-900/90' : 'border-white/70 bg-white/92 text-slate-700 hover:bg-white')}>
                  <X className="h-5 w-5" />
                </button>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>

          {activeRouteFalla && (
            <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} className={cn('pointer-events-auto absolute left-4 top-24 max-w-[28rem] rounded-[1.8rem] border px-4 py-4 shadow-[0_22px_48px_rgba(15,23,42,0.16)] backdrop-blur-2xl sm:left-5 sm:top-[6.4rem]', isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-slate-950/82 text-white' : 'border-white/70 bg-white/94 text-slate-950')}>
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
                <div className="min-w-0">
                  <span className="rounded-full bg-brand px-3 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-white">Ruta activa</span>
                  <p className="mt-3 text-[1.05rem] font-black leading-tight">{activeRouteFalla.name}</p>
                  <p className={cn('mt-1 text-sm font-bold', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/72' : 'text-slate-500')}>{activeRouteFalla.neighborhood}</p>
                </div>
                <div className="flex shrink-0 items-center gap-2">
                  <button type="button" onClick={() => handlePrepareRoute(activeRouteFalla)} className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-[1.15rem] bg-brand px-4 py-3 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-white shadow-[0_16px_30px_rgba(255,99,33,0.28)] transition-colors hover:bg-[#f45518]">
                    <Route className="h-4 w-4" />
                    Abrir guia
                  </button>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setActiveRouteFallaId(null)}
                    className={cn(
                      'inline-flex h-12 w-12 items-center justify-center rounded-[1.15rem] border transition-colors',
                      isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-white/8 text-white hover:bg-white/12' : 'border-slate-100 bg-slate-100 text-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-200'
                    )}
                    aria-label="Cerrar ruta"
                  >
                    <X className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </motion.div>
          )}

          {hasActivatedHeatmap && isHeatmapEnabled && (heatmapSummary.hottestZoneLabel || heatmapSummary.topFalla || heatmapSummary.topNeighborhood) ? (
            <motion.div
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 16 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              className={cn(
                'pointer-events-none absolute bottom-4 right-4 max-w-[20rem] rounded-[1.6rem] border px-4 py-4 shadow-[0_24px_54px_rgba(15,23,42,0.16)] backdrop-blur-2xl sm:bottom-5 sm:right-5',
                isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-slate-950/82 text-white' : 'border-white/80 bg-white/94 text-slate-950'
              )}
            >
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <span className="rounded-full bg-brand px-3 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-white">Actividad</span>
                {heatmapUpdatedLabel ? (
                  <span className={cn('text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em]', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/52' : 'text-slate-400')}>
                    {heatmapUpdatedLabel}
                  </span>
                ) : null}
              </div>
              <div className="mt-3 space-y-2.5">
                <div>
                  <p className={cn('text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em]', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/48' : 'text-slate-400')}>Zona más activa ahora</p>
                  <p className="mt-1 text-sm font-black">{heatmapSummary.hottestZoneLabel ?? 'Sin zona dominante'}</p>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className={cn('text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em]', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/48' : 'text-slate-400')}>Falla en tendencia</p>
                  <p className="mt-1 text-sm font-black">
                    {heatmapSummary.topFalla?.name || 'Sin tendencia clara'}
                  </p>
                  {heatmapSummary.topFalla?.sectionName ? (
                    <p className={cn('mt-1 text-[11px] font-bold', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/62' : 'text-slate-500')}>
                      {heatmapSummary.topFalla.sectionName}
                    </p>
                  ) : null}
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className={cn('text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em]', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/48' : 'text-slate-400')}>Barrio con más movimiento</p>
                  <p className="mt-1 text-sm font-black">{heatmapSummary.topNeighborhood?.name || 'Sin barrio destacado'}</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </motion.div>
          ) : null}

          <div className={cn('absolute inset-x-4 bottom-4 sm:bottom-5 sm:left-5 sm:right-auto', variant === 'expanded' ? 'sm:w-[24rem] lg:w-[26rem]' : 'sm:w-[22rem] lg:w-[24rem]')}>
            {selectedFalla || isIntroVisible ? (
              <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 18 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} key={selectedFalla?.id ?? 'map-intro'} className={cn('pointer-events-auto rounded-[2rem] border px-3.5 py-3.5 shadow-[0_30px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.18)] backdrop-blur-2xl', isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-slate-950/86 text-white' : 'border-white/80 bg-white/95 text-slate-950')}>
                {selectedFalla ? (
                  <>
                    <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
                      <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                        <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                          <span className="rounded-full bg-brand px-3 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-white">{selectedFalla.section}</span>
                          {selectedFalla.prize && <span className="rounded-full bg-amber-400 px-3 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-amber-950">#{selectedFalla.prize} premio</span>}
                        </div>
                        <h3 className="mt-3 text-[1.45rem] font-black leading-[1.02] tracking-tight">{selectedFalla.name}</h3>
                        <p className={cn('mt-2 text-sm font-bold', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/72' : 'text-slate-500')}>{selectedFalla.neighborhood} | {selectedFalla.artist}</p>
                      </div>
                      <button type="button" onClick={(event) => handleFavoriteToggle(selectedFalla, event)} className={cn('pointer-events-auto inline-flex h-12 w-12 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-[1.15rem] border transition-colors', favorites.includes(selectedFalla.id) ? 'border-red-200 bg-red-500 text-white' : isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-white/8 text-white hover:bg-white/12' : 'border-slate-100 bg-slate-100 text-slate-500 hover:bg-slate-200')}>
                        <Heart className={cn('h-5 w-5', favorites.includes(selectedFalla.id) && 'fill-current')} />
                      </button>
                    </div>
                    <p className={cn('mt-4 text-sm font-bold leading-6', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/72' : 'text-slate-600')}>{selectedFalla.description}</p>
                    <div className="mt-4 grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
                      <div className={cn('rounded-[1.2rem] px-3 py-3', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-white/8' : 'bg-[#fff6ef]')}><p className={cn('text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em]', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/48' : 'text-brand')}>Barrio</p><p className="mt-2 text-sm font-black">{selectedFalla.neighborhood}</p></div>
                      <div className={cn('rounded-[1.2rem] px-3 py-3', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-white/8' : 'bg-[#fff6ef]')}><p className={cn('text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em]', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/48' : 'text-brand')}>Likes</p><p className="mt-2 text-sm font-black">{selectedFalla.likes}</p></div>
                      <div className={cn('rounded-[1.2rem] px-3 py-3', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-white/8' : 'bg-[#fff6ef]')}><p className={cn('text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em]', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/48' : 'text-brand')}>Visitas</p><p className="mt-2 text-sm font-black">{selectedFalla.visitors}</p></div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="mt-4 grid gap-2 sm:grid-cols-[1fr_1fr_auto]">
                      <button type="button" onClick={() => handleShowDetail(selectedFalla)} className={cn('pointer-events-auto inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-[1.2rem] px-4 py-3 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-colors', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-white text-slate-950 hover:bg-slate-100' : 'bg-slate-950 text-white hover:bg-slate-800')}><Eye className="h-4 w-4" />Ver detalle</button>
                      <button type="button" onClick={() => handlePrepareRoute(selectedFalla)} className="pointer-events-auto inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-[1.2rem] bg-brand px-4 py-3 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-white shadow-[0_16px_30px_rgba(255,99,33,0.28)] transition-colors hover:bg-[#f45518]"><Route className="h-4 w-4" />Preparar ruta</button>
                      <button type="button" onClick={() => { setSelectedFalla(null); setActiveRouteFallaId(null); }} className={cn('pointer-events-auto inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-[1.2rem] px-4 py-3 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-colors', isDarkTheme ? 'bg-white/10 text-white hover:bg-white/14' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-200')}>Limpiar</button>
                    </div>
                  </>
                ) : (
                  <>
                    <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
                      <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full bg-brand/12 px-3 py-1.5 text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-brand"><Sparkles className="h-3 w-3" />Mapa fallero</div>
                      <button
                        type="button"
                        onClick={() => setIsIntroVisible(false)}
                        className={cn(
                          'pointer-events-auto inline-flex h-9 w-9 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-[1rem] border transition-colors',
                          isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-white/8 text-white hover:bg-white/12' : 'border-slate-100 bg-slate-100 text-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-200'
                        )}
                        aria-label="Ocultar panel"
                      >
                        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
                      </button>
                    </div>
                    <h3 className="mt-2.5 text-[1.35rem] font-black leading-[1.05] tracking-tight">Decide ruta sin salir del mapa.</h3>
                    <p className={cn('mt-2 text-[13px] font-bold leading-5', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/72' : 'text-slate-600')}>
                      {mapSearchQuery ? `Resultados para "${mapSearchQuery}".` : 'Selecciona una falla para abrir su ficha, guardar favoritos o preparar la navegacion desde el propio mapa.'}
                    </p>
                    {quickFallas.length > 0 ? (
                      <div className="mt-3 grid gap-2">
                        {quickFallas.map((falla) => (
                          <button key={falla.id} type="button" onClick={() => handleMarkerSelect(falla)} className={cn('pointer-events-auto flex items-center justify-between gap-3 rounded-[1.3rem] border px-3 py-2.5 text-left transition-colors', isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/10 bg-white/8 hover:bg-white/12' : 'border-white/80 bg-white hover:bg-[#fff7f1]')}>
                            <div className="min-w-0">
                              <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                                <p className="text-[13px] font-black line-clamp-1">{falla.name}</p>
                                {falla.prize && (
                                  <span className="rounded-full bg-amber-400 px-2 py-0.5 text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-amber-950">
                                    #{falla.prize}
                                  </span>
                                )}
                              </div>
                              <p className={cn('mt-1 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.14em]', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/48' : 'text-slate-400')}>
                                {falla.neighborhood} | {userPosition ? formatDistance(distanceBetweenPoints(userPosition, [falla.lat, falla.lng])) : falla.prize ? `#${falla.prize} premio` : `${falla.likes} likes`}
                              </p>
                            </div>
                            <ArrowRight className="h-3.5 w-3.5 shrink-0 text-brand" />
                          </button>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    ) : (
                      <div className={cn('mt-3 rounded-[1.4rem] border px-3.5 py-3.5', isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/10 bg-white/8' : 'border-white/80 bg-white')}>
                        <p className="text-[13px] font-black">No hay coincidencias en el mapa.</p>
                        <p className={cn('mt-1 text-[11px] font-bold leading-5', isDarkTheme ? 'text-white/60' : 'text-slate-500')}>
                          Prueba con otro nombre o limpia la busqueda para volver a ver todas las fallas.
                        </p>
                        {mapSearchQuery ? (
                          <button
                            type="button"
                            onClick={() => setMapSearchQuery('')}
                            className="mt-3 inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-[1rem] bg-brand px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-white"
                          >
                            Limpiar busqueda
                          </button>
                        ) : null}
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </>
                )}
              </motion.div>
            ) : (
              <motion.button
                type="button"
                initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 18 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                onClick={() => setIsIntroVisible(true)}
                className={cn(
                  'pointer-events-auto inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full border px-4 py-3 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] shadow-[0_20px_44px_rgba(15,23,42,0.15)] backdrop-blur-2xl transition-colors',
                  isDarkTheme ? 'border-white/12 bg-slate-950/82 text-white hover:bg-slate-900/90' : 'border-white/80 bg-white/94 text-slate-700 hover:bg-white'
                )}
              >
                <Sparkles className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-brand" />
                Mostrar panel
              </motion.button>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  );
}

function areFallaMapPropsEqual(previous: FallaMapProps, next: FallaMapProps) {
  const previousUserPosition = previous.userPosition;
  const nextUserPosition = next.userPosition;

  return (
    previous.isDarkMode === next.isDarkMode
    && previous.variant === next.variant
    && previous.frameClassName === next.frameClassName
    && previous.mapHeightClassName === next.mapHeightClassName
    && previous.heatmapEnabled === next.heatmapEnabled
    && previous.setHeatmapEnabled === next.setHeatmapEnabled
    && previous.mapStyleId === next.mapStyleId
    && previous.mapSearchQuery === next.mapSearchQuery
    && previous.onOpenExpandedMap === next.onOpenExpandedMap
    && previous.activeRouteFallaId === next.activeRouteFallaId
    && previous.activeRouteFalla?.id === next.activeRouteFalla?.id
    && previous.fallas === next.fallas
    && previous.selectedFalla?.id === next.selectedFalla?.id
    && previous.locationStatus === next.locationStatus
    && previous.favorites === next.favorites
    && previousUserPosition?.[0] === nextUserPosition?.[0]
    && previousUserPosition?.[1] === nextUserPosition?.[1]
  );
}

export const FallaMap = React.memo(FallaMapComponent, areFallaMapPropsEqual);
FallaMap.displayName = 'FallaMap';

interface ActivityItemProps {

function resolveIcon(eventType: string) {
  if (eventType.includes('badge')) {
    return Trophy;
  }
  if (eventType.includes('route')) {
    return Route;
  }
  if (eventType.includes('favorite')) {
    return Heart;
  }
  if (eventType.includes('navigation')) {
    return Compass;
  }
  if (eventType.includes('visit')) {
    return Sparkles;
  }

  return CalendarDays;
}

export const ActivityItem: FC<ActivityItemProps> = ({ item, isDarkMode }) => {
  const Icon = resolveIcon(item.eventType);

  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        'flex items-start gap-3 rounded-[1.3rem] border px-4 py-3',
        isDarkMode ? 'border-white/10 bg-white/[0.045]' : 'border-slate-100 bg-white'
      )}
    >
      <div className={cn('flex h-10 w-10 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-[1rem]', isDarkMode ? 'bg-brand/16 text-brand' : 'bg-brand/10 text-brand')}>
        <Icon className="h-4 w-4" />
      </div>
      <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
        <p className="text-sm font-black leading-5">{item.title}</p>
        <p className="mt-1 text-sm font-bold leading-6 opacity-65">{item.body}</p>
      </div>
      <span className="shrink-0 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] opacity-45">
        {item.occurredAt ? new Date(item.occurredAt.replace(' ', 'T')).toLocaleDateString('es-ES', { day: '2-digit', month: 'short' }) : ''}
